12:T46fd8,<h1 id="multi-agent-协作的基石协议标准化探索之路">Multi-Agent
协作的基石：协议标准化探索之路</h1>
<blockquote>
<p>基于 Google Gemini CLI 和 OpenAI Codex 源码的深度技术剖析</p>
<p><strong>源码版本说明</strong> 本文基于以下版本的源码分析：</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Gemini CLI</strong>: v0.10.0-nightly (2025-10-13)</li>
<li><strong>Codex CLI</strong>: v0.2.0-alpha.2 (2025-11-25)</li>
<li><strong>MCP 协议</strong>: 2025-06-18 规范</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="摘要">摘要</h2>
<ul>
<li>随着 AI Agent 的快速发展，如何让不同的 Agent
之间高效协作、如何标准化 Agent
与外部工具的交互，已成为业界关注的焦点。</li>
<li>本文通过深入分析 <strong>Google Gemini CLI</strong> 和
<strong>OpenAI Codex</strong> 的源码实现，对比两大主流协议——<strong>MCP
(Model Context Protocol)</strong> 和 <strong>ACP (Agent Context
Protocol)</strong> 的设计理念、技术架构和应用场景，并探讨 AI Agent
协议的未来发展方向。</li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h2
id="一协议背景为什么需要标准化">一、协议背景：为什么需要标准化？</h2>
<h3 id="11-当前-ai-agent-生态的痛点">1.1 当前 AI Agent 生态的痛点</h3>
<p>在协议标准化之前，AI Agent 面临以下核心挑战：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>痛点</th>
<th>描述</th>
<th>影响</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>孤岛效应</strong></td>
<td>每个 Agent 使用私有协议，无法互操作</td>
<td>无法构建 Multi-Agent 系统</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>工具集成困难</strong></td>
<td>每个工具需要为不同 Agent 重复开发适配器</td>
<td>开发成本高，生态碎片化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>状态不可恢复</strong></td>
<td>会话状态无法持久化或跨系统传递</td>
<td>用户体验差，无法长期任务</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>安全性缺失</strong></td>
<td>缺乏统一的权限控制和审计机制</td>
<td>企业级部署存在风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 id="12-协议标准化的价值">1.2 协议标准化的价值</h3>
<pre class="mermaid"><code>graph TB
    subgraph before[&quot;标准化前：N × M 问题&quot;]
        A1[&quot;Agent1&quot;] --&gt; T1A[&quot;Tool1 (适配器 1-1)&quot;]
        A1 --&gt; T2A[&quot;Tool2 (适配器 1-2)&quot;]
        A1 --&gt; T3A[&quot;Tool3 (适配器 1-3)&quot;]

        A2[&quot;Agent2&quot;] --&gt; T1B[&quot;Tool1 (适配器 2-1)&quot;]
        A2 --&gt; T2B[&quot;Tool2 (适配器 2-2)&quot;]
        A2 --&gt; T3B[&quot;Tool3 (适配器 2-3)&quot;]

        style before fill:#ffebee,stroke:#c62828
    end

    subgraph after[&quot;标准化后：N + M 问题&quot;]
        Agent1[&quot;Agent1&quot;] --&gt; Protocol[&quot;MCP\u002FACP 协议层&quot;]
        Agent2[&quot;Agent2&quot;] --&gt; Protocol
        Agent3[&quot;Agent3&quot;] --&gt; Protocol

        Protocol --&gt; Tool1[&quot;Tool1&quot;]
        Protocol --&gt; Tool2[&quot;Tool2&quot;]
        Protocol --&gt; Tool3[&quot;Tool3&quot;]

        style after fill:#e8f5e9,stroke:#2e7d32
        style Protocol fill:#fff3e0,stroke:#e65100
    end</code></pre>
<p><strong>对比结果</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>标准化前</strong>: 需要 <strong>N × M</strong> 个适配器
(每个 Agent 为每个 Tool 开发专用适配器)</li>
<li><strong>标准化后</strong>: 仅需 <strong>N + M</strong> 个适配器
(Agent 实现协议 + Tool 实现协议)</li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h2 id="二mcp-model-context-protocol-深度解析">二、MCP (Model Context
Protocol) 深度解析</h2>
<h3 id="21-mcp-协议概述">2.1 MCP 协议概述</h3>
<p><strong>MCP</strong> 由 Anthropic 提出，是一个专注于 <strong>Agent
与外部工具\u002F资源交互</strong> 的标准协议。</p>
<p><strong>核心设计理念</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>📦 <strong>资源抽象</strong>:
将外部系统（数据库、API、文件系统）抽象为统一的 Resource</li>
<li>🔧 <strong>工具调用</strong>: 标准化的工具发现、调用和响应流程</li>
<li>🔌 <strong>传输无关</strong>: 支持 stdio、SSE、HTTP
等多种传输方式</li>
<li>🔐 <strong>权限控制</strong>: 内置的工具执行审批机制</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>协议版本</strong>: <code>2025-06-18</code> (来源: Codex
<code>mcp-types\u002Fsrc\u002Flib.rs</code>)</p>
<h3 id="22-gemini-cli-的-mcp-实现架构">2.2 Gemini CLI 的 MCP
实现架构</h3>
<h4 id="核心组件"><strong>核心组件</strong>:</h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb2"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb2-1"><a href="#cb2-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F packages\u002Fcore\u002Fsrc\u002Ftools\u002Fmcp<span class="op">-</span>client<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">ts</span></span>
<span id="cb2-2"><a href="#cb2-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="im">export</span> <span class="kw">class</span> McpClient {</span>
<span id="cb2-3"><a href="#cb2-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">private</span> client<span class="op">:</span> Client<span class="op">;</span>                    \u002F\u002F MCP SDK Client</span>
<span id="cb2-4"><a href="#cb2-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">private</span> transport<span class="op">:</span> Transport<span class="op">;</span>              \u002F\u002F <span class="fu">传输层</span> (stdio\u002FSSE\u002FHTTP)</span>
<span id="cb2-5"><a href="#cb2-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">private</span> status<span class="op">:</span> MCPServerStatus<span class="op">;</span>           \u002F\u002F 连接状态</span>
<span id="cb2-6"><a href="#cb2-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb2-7"><a href="#cb2-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="fu">connect</span>()<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dt">void</span><span class="op">&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb2-8"><a href="#cb2-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">1.</span> 建立传输连接</span>
<span id="cb2-9"><a href="#cb2-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">transport</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fu">createTransport</span>(<span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">serverConfig</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-10"><a href="#cb2-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb2-11"><a href="#cb2-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">2.</span> 初始化 MCP Client</span>
<span id="cb2-12"><a href="#cb2-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">client</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fu">Client</span>({</span>
<span id="cb2-13"><a href="#cb2-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;gemini-cli&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb2-14"><a href="#cb2-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      version<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;0.10.0&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-15"><a href="#cb2-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }<span class="op">,</span> {</span>
<span id="cb2-16"><a href="#cb2-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      capabilities<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb2-17"><a href="#cb2-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        roots<span class="op">:</span> { listChanged<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">true</span> }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb2-18"><a href="#cb2-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        sampling<span class="op">:</span> {}</span>
<span id="cb2-19"><a href="#cb2-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      }</span>
<span id="cb2-20"><a href="#cb2-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    })<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-21"><a href="#cb2-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb2-22"><a href="#cb2-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">3.</span> 连接到 MCP <span class="bu">Server</span></span>
<span id="cb2-23"><a href="#cb2-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">client</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">connect</span>(<span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">transport</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-24"><a href="#cb2-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb2-25"><a href="#cb2-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb2-26"><a href="#cb2-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="fu">discover</span>()<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dt">void</span><span class="op">&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb2-27"><a href="#cb2-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F 发现工具</span>
<span id="cb2-28"><a href="#cb2-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> tools <span class="op">=</span> <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">client</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">listTools</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-29"><a href="#cb2-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb2-30"><a href="#cb2-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F 发现资源</span>
<span id="cb2-31"><a href="#cb2-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> resources <span class="op">=</span> <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">client</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">listResources</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-32"><a href="#cb2-32" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb2-33"><a href="#cb2-33" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F 发现 Prompts</span>
<span id="cb2-34"><a href="#cb2-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> prompts <span class="op">=</span> <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">client</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">listPrompts</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-35"><a href="#cb2-35" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb2-36"><a href="#cb2-36" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<h4 id="工具调用流程"><strong>工具调用流程</strong>:</h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb3"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb3-1"><a href="#cb3-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F packages\u002Fcore\u002Fsrc\u002Ftools\u002Fmcp<span class="op">-</span>tool<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">ts</span></span>
<span id="cb3-2"><a href="#cb3-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">class</span> DiscoveredMCPToolInvocation {</span>
<span id="cb3-3"><a href="#cb3-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="fu">execute</span>(signal<span class="op">:</span> AbortSignal)<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">&lt;</span>ToolResult<span class="op">&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb3-4"><a href="#cb3-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">1.</span> 检查是否需要用户批准</span>

<span id="cb3-6"><a href="#cb3-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span> (confirmationDetails) {</span>
<span id="cb3-7"><a href="#cb3-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">waitForUserApproval</span>(confirmationDetails)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-8"><a href="#cb3-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb3-9"><a href="#cb3-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb3-10"><a href="#cb3-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">2.</span> 调用 MCP Tool</span>
<span id="cb3-11"><a href="#cb3-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> functionCalls<span class="op">:</span> FunctionCall[] <span class="op">=</span> [{</span>
<span id="cb3-12"><a href="#cb3-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">serverToolName</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb3-13"><a href="#cb3-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      args<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">params</span></span>
<span id="cb3-14"><a href="#cb3-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }]<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-15"><a href="#cb3-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb3-16"><a href="#cb3-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> rawResponseParts <span class="op">=</span> <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">mcpTool</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">callToolBatch</span>(</span>
<span id="cb3-17"><a href="#cb3-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      functionCalls<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb3-18"><a href="#cb3-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      signal</span>
<span id="cb3-19"><a href="#cb3-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    )<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-20"><a href="#cb3-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb3-21"><a href="#cb3-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">3.</span> 处理响应</span>
<span id="cb3-22"><a href="#cb3-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">parseToolResponse</span>(rawResponseParts)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-23"><a href="#cb3-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>

<h3 id="23-codex-的-mcp-实现架构">2.3 Codex 的 MCP 实现架构</h3>

<div class="sourceCode" id="cb4"><pre
class="sourceCode rust"><code class="sourceCode rust"><span id="cb4-1"><a href="#cb4-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F codex<span class="op">-</span>rs\u002Fcore\u002Fsrc\u002Fmcp_connection_manager<span class="op">.</span>rs</span>
<span id="cb4-2"><a href="#cb4-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">pub</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> McpConnectionManager <span class="op">{</span></span>
<span id="cb4-3"><a href="#cb4-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    clients<span class="op">:</span> HashMap<span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dt">String</span><span class="op">,</span> AsyncManagedClient<span class="op">&gt;,</span></span>

<span id="cb4-8"><a href="#cb4-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">impl</span> McpConnectionManager <span class="op">{</span></span>
<span id="cb4-9"><a href="#cb4-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">pub</span> <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">fn</span> connect_server(</span>
<span id="cb4-10"><a href="#cb4-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="op">&amp;</span><span class="kw">self</span><span class="op">,</span></span>

<span id="cb4-14"><a href="#cb4-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        \u002F\u002F <span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">.</span> 创建 RmcpClient (Rust MCP Client)</span>
<span id="cb4-15"><a href="#cb4-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="kw">let</span> client <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">RmcpClient::</span>new(</span>
<span id="cb4-16"><a href="#cb4-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            Implementation <span class="op">{</span></span>
<span id="cb4-17"><a href="#cb4-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;codex&quot;</span><span class="op">.</span>to_string()<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb4-18"><a href="#cb4-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                version<span class="op">:</span> <span class="pp">env!</span>(<span class="st">&quot;CARGO_PKG_VERSION&quot;</span>)<span class="op">.</span>to_string()<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb4-19"><a href="#cb4-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="op">},</span></span>
<span id="cb4-20"><a href="#cb4-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            ClientCapabilities <span class="op">{</span></span>
<span id="cb4-21"><a href="#cb4-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                roots<span class="op">:</span> <span class="cn">Some</span>(RootsCapability <span class="op">{</span> list_changed<span class="op">:</span> <span class="cn">true</span> <span class="op">}</span>)<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb4-22"><a href="#cb4-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                sampling<span class="op">:</span> <span class="cn">Some</span>(SamplingCapability <span class="op">{}</span>)<span class="op">,</span></span>

<span id="cb4-24"><a href="#cb4-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        )<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb4-27"><a href="#cb4-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="kw">let</span> transport <span class="op">=</span> <span class="cf">match</span> <span class="op">&amp;</span>config<span class="op">.</span>transport <span class="op">{</span></span>

<h4 id="工具名称限定-fully-qualified-names"><strong>工具名称限定 (Fully
Qualified Names)</strong>:</h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb5"><pre
class="sourceCode rust"><code class="sourceCode rust"><span id="cb5-1"><a href="#cb5-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F codex<span class="op">-</span>rs\u002Fcore\u002Fsrc\u002Fmcp_connection_manager<span class="op">.</span>rs</span>
<span id="cb5-2"><a href="#cb5-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> MCP_TOOL_NAME_DELIMITER<span class="op">:</span> <span class="op">&amp;</span><span class="dt">str</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;__&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-3"><a href="#cb5-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> MAX_TOOL_NAME_LENGTH<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">usize</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">64</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-4"><a href="#cb5-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb5-5"><a href="#cb5-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">fn</span> qualify_tools(tools<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">Vec</span><span class="op">&lt;</span>ToolInfo<span class="op">&gt;</span>) <span class="op">-&gt;</span> HashMap<span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dt">String</span><span class="op">,</span> ToolInfo<span class="op">&gt;</span> <span class="op">{</span></span>
<span id="cb5-6"><a href="#cb5-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="kw">mut</span> qualified_tools <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">HashMap::</span>new()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-7"><a href="#cb5-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb5-8"><a href="#cb5-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">for</span> tool <span class="kw">in</span> tools <span class="op">{</span></span>
<span id="cb5-9"><a href="#cb5-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        \u002F\u002F 格式<span class="op">:</span> mcp__<span class="op">&lt;</span>server_name<span class="op">&gt;</span>__<span class="op">&lt;</span>tool_name<span class="op">&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-10"><a href="#cb5-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="kw">let</span> qualified_name <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">format!</span>(</span>
<span id="cb5-11"><a href="#cb5-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="st">&quot;mcp{}{}{}{}&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb5-12"><a href="#cb5-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            MCP_TOOL_NAME_DELIMITER<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb5-13"><a href="#cb5-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            tool<span class="op">.</span>server_name<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb5-14"><a href="#cb5-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            MCP_TOOL_NAME_DELIMITER<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb5-15"><a href="#cb5-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            tool<span class="op">.</span>tool_name</span>
<span id="cb5-16"><a href="#cb5-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        )<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-17"><a href="#cb5-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb5-18"><a href="#cb5-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        \u002F\u002F 超长则使用 SHA1 截断</span>
<span id="cb5-19"><a href="#cb5-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">if</span> qualified_name<span class="op">.</span>len() <span class="op">&gt;</span> MAX_TOOL_NAME_LENGTH <span class="op">{</span></span>
<span id="cb5-20"><a href="#cb5-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="kw">let</span> hash <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">sha1::Sha1::</span>digest(qualified_name<span class="op">.</span>as_bytes())<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-21"><a href="#cb5-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            qualified_name <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">format!</span>(<span class="st">&quot;{}_{:x}&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb5-22"><a href="#cb5-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                <span class="op">&amp;</span>qualified_name[<span class="op">..</span><span class="dv">48</span>]<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb5-23"><a href="#cb5-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                hash</span>
<span id="cb5-24"><a href="#cb5-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            )<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-25"><a href="#cb5-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="op">}</span></span>
<span id="cb5-26"><a href="#cb5-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb5-27"><a href="#cb5-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        qualified_tools<span class="op">.</span>insert(qualified_name<span class="op">,</span> tool)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-28"><a href="#cb5-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="op">}</span></span>
<span id="cb5-29"><a href="#cb5-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb5-30"><a href="#cb5-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    qualified_tools</span>
<span id="cb5-31"><a href="#cb5-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="op">}</span></span></code></pre></div>
<h3 id="24-mcp-协议消息示例">2.4 MCP 协议消息示例</h3>

<hr />
<h2 id="三acp-agent-client-protocol-官方标准深度解析">三、ACP (Agent
Client Protocol) 官方标准深度解析</h2>
<h3 id="31-acp-协议概述">3.1 ACP 协议概述</h3>
<p><strong>ACP (Agent Client Protocol)</strong> 是由 <strong>Zed
Industries</strong> 在 <strong>2025 年 8
月</strong>正式发布的开放标准，旨在标准化<strong>代码编辑器\u002FIDE 与
AI 编码代理之间的通信</strong>。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>📖 <strong>官方资源</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>官网：<a
href="https:\u002F\u002Fagentclientprotocol.com\u002F">https:\u002F\u002Fagentclientprotocol.com\u002F</a></li>
<li>GitHub：<a
href="https:\u002F\u002Fgithub.com\u002Fagentclientprotocol\u002Fagent-client-protocol">https:\u002F\u002Fgithub.com\u002Fagentclientprotocol\u002Fagent-client-protocol</a></li>
<li>TypeScript SDK：<code>@agentclientprotocol\u002Fsdk</code>
(npm)</li>
<li>协议版本：<strong>Version 1</strong> (当前)</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>核心定位</strong>: ACP 类似于 <strong>LSP (Language Server
Protocol)</strong> 在语言服务器领域的作用，解决了 Agent-Editor 集成的
<strong>N×M 问题</strong>：</p>
<pre class="mermaid"><code>graph LR
    subgraph before[&quot;ACP 之前：N × M 集成问题&quot;]
        E1[&quot;Editor1&quot;] --&gt; A1A[&quot;Agent1 (定制集成)&quot;]
        E1 --&gt; A2A[&quot;Agent2 (定制集成)&quot;]
        E1 --&gt; A3A[&quot;Agent3 (定制集成)&quot;]

        E2[&quot;Editor2&quot;] --&gt; A1B[&quot;Agent1 (重复开发)&quot;]
        E2 --&gt; A2B[&quot;Agent2 (重复开发)&quot;]

        style before fill:#ffebee,stroke:#c62828
    end

    subgraph after[&quot;ACP 之后：N + M 标准化&quot;]
        Editor1[&quot;Editor1&quot;] --&gt; ACP[&quot;ACP 协议层&quot;]
        Editor2[&quot;Editor2&quot;] --&gt; ACP
        Editor3[&quot;Editor3&quot;] --&gt; ACP

        ACP --&gt; Agent1[&quot;Agent1&quot;]
        ACP --&gt; Agent2[&quot;Agent2&quot;]
        ACP --&gt; Agent3[&quot;Agent3&quot;]

        style after fill:#e8f5e9,stroke:#2e7d32
        style ACP fill:#e3f2fd,stroke:#1565c0
    end</code></pre>
<p><strong>核心设计理念</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>📝 <strong>标准化通信</strong>: 基于 JSON-RPC 2.0，使用 stdio
传输</li>
<li>🔌 <strong>即插即用</strong>: 任何支持 ACP 的编辑器都能使用任何 ACP
代理</li>
<li>🎯 <strong>代理自主性</strong>:
代理作为编辑器的子进程运行，可自主修改代码</li>
<li>🔐 <strong>权限控制</strong>:
明确的权限请求机制（文件系统、终端等）</li>
<li>🔄 <strong>会话管理</strong>: 支持会话创建、加载、状态追踪</li>
<li>📊 <strong>能力协商</strong>: 初始化时协商双方支持的功能</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="32-acp-协议架构">3.2 ACP 协议架构</h3>
<h4 id="通信模型"><strong>通信模型</strong></h4>
<p>ACP 遵循 <strong>JSON-RPC 2.0</strong> 规范，定义了两种消息类型：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>消息类型</th>
<th>描述</th>
<th>是否需要响应</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>Methods</strong></td>
<td>请求-响应对，期望返回结果或错误</td>
<td>✅ 是</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Notifications</strong></td>
<td>单向消息，用于事件通知</td>
<td>❌ 否</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h4 id="角色定义"><strong>角色定义</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb11"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb11-1"><a href="#cb11-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F Agent：使用生成式 AI 自主修改代码的程序</span>
<span id="cb11-2"><a href="#cb11-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">interface</span> Agent {</span>
<span id="cb11-3"><a href="#cb11-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="op">===</span> 基线方法（必须实现） <span class="op">===</span></span>
<span id="cb11-4"><a href="#cb11-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">initialize</span>()<span class="op">:</span> InitializeResult<span class="op">;</span>           \u002F\u002F 初始化和能力协商</span>
<span id="cb11-5"><a href="#cb11-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  authenticate<span class="op">?</span>()<span class="op">:</span> AuthResult<span class="op">;</span>              \u002F\u002F 身份验证（可选）</span>
<span id="cb11-6"><a href="#cb11-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">new&#39;</span>()<span class="op">:</span> SessionId<span class="op">;</span>              \u002F\u002F 创建新会话</span>
<span id="cb11-7"><a href="#cb11-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">prompt&#39;</span>(msg<span class="op">:</span> Message)<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">void</span><span class="op">;</span>    \u002F\u002F 接收用户提示词</span>
<span id="cb11-8"><a href="#cb11-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb11-9"><a href="#cb11-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="op">===</span> 可选方法 <span class="op">===</span></span>
<span id="cb11-10"><a href="#cb11-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">load&#39;</span><span class="op">?</span>(id<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">string</span>)<span class="op">:</span> Session<span class="op">;</span>    \u002F\u002F 加载已有会话</span>
<span id="cb11-11"><a href="#cb11-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">set_mode&#39;</span><span class="op">?</span>(mode<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">string</span>)<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">void</span><span class="op">;</span> \u002F\u002F 设置模式（如 edit\u002Fchat）</span>
<span id="cb11-12"><a href="#cb11-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb11-13"><a href="#cb11-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="op">===</span> 通知 <span class="op">===</span></span>
<span id="cb11-14"><a href="#cb11-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">cancel&#39;</span>()<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">void</span><span class="op">;</span>                \u002F\u002F 取消当前操作</span>
<span id="cb11-15"><a href="#cb11-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb11-16"><a href="#cb11-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb11-17"><a href="#cb11-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F Client：提供用户界面的代码编辑器\u002FIDE</span>
<span id="cb11-18"><a href="#cb11-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">interface</span> Client {</span>
<span id="cb11-19"><a href="#cb11-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="op">===</span> 基线方法（必须实现） <span class="op">===</span></span>
<span id="cb11-20"><a href="#cb11-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">request_permission&#39;</span>(req<span class="op">:</span> PermissionRequest)<span class="op">:</span> PermissionResult<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb11-21"><a href="#cb11-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb11-22"><a href="#cb11-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="op">===</span> 可选方法（根据能力） <span class="op">===</span></span>
<span id="cb11-23"><a href="#cb11-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;fs</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">read_text_file&#39;</span><span class="op">?</span>(path<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">string</span>)<span class="op">:</span> string<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb11-24"><a href="#cb11-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;fs</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">write_text_file&#39;</span><span class="op">?</span>(path<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">string</span><span class="op">,</span> content<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">string</span>)<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">void</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb11-25"><a href="#cb11-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;terminal</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">create&#39;</span><span class="op">?</span>(cmd<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">string</span>)<span class="op">:</span> TerminalId<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb11-26"><a href="#cb11-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;terminal</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">output&#39;</span><span class="op">?</span>(id<span class="op">:</span> TerminalId)<span class="op">:</span> TerminalOutput<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb11-27"><a href="#cb11-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb11-28"><a href="#cb11-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="op">===</span> 通知 <span class="op">===</span></span>
<span id="cb11-29"><a href="#cb11-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&#39;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">update&#39;</span>(update<span class="op">:</span> SessionUpdate)<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">void</span><span class="op">;</span>  \u002F\u002F 会话状态更新</span>
<span id="cb11-30"><a href="#cb11-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<h3 id="33-acp-核心流程">3.3 ACP 核心流程</h3>
<h4 id="1-初始化流程"><strong>1. 初始化流程</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb12"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb12-1"><a href="#cb12-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F Client → Agent</span>
<span id="cb12-2"><a href="#cb12-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>{</span>
<span id="cb12-3"><a href="#cb12-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;jsonrpc&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;2.0&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb12-4"><a href="#cb12-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;id&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb12-5"><a href="#cb12-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;method&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;initialize&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb12-6"><a href="#cb12-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;params&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> {</span>

<span id="cb12-48"><a href="#cb12-48" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>关键要求</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>🔢 <strong>协议版本协商</strong>: Client 提供支持的最新版本，Agent
响应选定版本</li>
<li>🎛️ <strong>能力声明</strong>:
双方明确声明支持的功能（文件系统、终端、MCP 等）</li>
<li>⚙️ <strong>向后兼容</strong>: 未声明的能力视为不支持</li>
</ul>

<span id="cb14-56"><a href="#cb14-56" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;jsonrpc&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;2.0&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb14-57"><a href="#cb14-57" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;id&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="dv">100</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb14-58"><a href="#cb14-58" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;result&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb14-59"><a href="#cb14-59" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="st">&quot;granted&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">true</span></span>
<span id="cb14-60"><a href="#cb14-60" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb14-61"><a href="#cb14-61" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb14-62"><a href="#cb14-62" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb14-63"><a href="#cb14-63" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F Agent → Client<span class="op">:</span> 完成状态</span>
<span id="cb14-64"><a href="#cb14-64" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>{</span>
<span id="cb14-65"><a href="#cb14-65" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;jsonrpc&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;2.0&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb14-66"><a href="#cb14-66" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;method&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;session</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">update&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb14-67"><a href="#cb14-67" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="st">&quot;params&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb14-68"><a href="#cb14-68" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="st">&quot;sessionId&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;sess_abc123&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb14-69"><a href="#cb14-69" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="st">&quot;update&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb14-70"><a href="#cb14-70" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&quot;kind&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;state_change&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb14-71"><a href="#cb14-71" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&quot;state&quot;</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;completed&quot;</span></span>
<span id="cb14-72"><a href="#cb14-72" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb14-73"><a href="#cb14-73" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb14-74"><a href="#cb14-74" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>

<h3 id="35-acp-协议约定">3.5 ACP 协议约定</h3>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb15"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb15-1"><a href="#cb15-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F 关键约定</span>
<span id="cb15-2"><a href="#cb15-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> ACP_CONVENTIONS <span class="op">=</span> {</span>
<span id="cb15-3"><a href="#cb15-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">1.</span> 路径要求</span>
<span id="cb15-4"><a href="#cb15-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  filePaths<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;MUST be absolute&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span>  \u002F\u002F 所有文件路径必须是绝对路径</span>
<span id="cb15-5"><a href="#cb15-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb15-6"><a href="#cb15-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">2.</span> 行号约定</span>
<span id="cb15-7"><a href="#cb15-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  lineNumbers<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;1-based&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span>  \u002F\u002F 行号从 <span class="dv">1</span> 开始</span>
<span id="cb15-8"><a href="#cb15-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb15-9"><a href="#cb15-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">3.</span> 文本格式</span>
<span id="cb15-10"><a href="#cb15-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  textFormat<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;Markdown&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span>  \u002F\u002F 默认使用 Markdown 格式</span>
<span id="cb15-11"><a href="#cb15-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb15-12"><a href="#cb15-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">4.</span> 扩展机制</span>
<span id="cb15-13"><a href="#cb15-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  customMethods<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;prefix with underscore (_method_name)&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb15-14"><a href="#cb15-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  customData<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;use _meta field&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb15-15"><a href="#cb15-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb15-16"><a href="#cb15-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">5.</span> 错误处理</span>
<span id="cb15-17"><a href="#cb15-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  errorHandling<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;JSON-RPC 2.0 standard (code + message)&quot;</span></span>
<span id="cb15-18"><a href="#cb15-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<hr />
<h2 id="四a2a-agent-to-agent-深度剖析multi-agent-系统的探索">四、A2A
(Agent-to-Agent) 深度剖析：Multi-Agent 系统的探索</h2>
<h3 id="40-a2a-概述与设计哲学">4.0 A2A 概述与设计哲学</h3>
<p><strong>A2A (Agent-to-Agent Protocol)</strong> 是 Google Gemini CLI
团队提出的实验性协议，专注于解决 <strong>Multi-Agent
系统</strong>中的核心挑战：如何让不同的 Agent
无缝协作、状态同步和任务编排。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>🎯 <strong>核心价值主张</strong></p>
<p>虽然 ACP 解决了 Editor ↔︎ Agent 的标准化，MCP 解决了 Agent ↔︎ Tools
的标准化，但 <strong>Agent ↔︎ Agent</strong> 的协作仍是空白地带。A2A
正是为填补这一空白而生。</p>
</blockquote>
<h4 id="a2a-的三大设计支柱"><strong>A2A 的三大设计支柱</strong></h4>
<pre class="mermaid"><code>graph TD
    A2A[&quot;A2A 设计哲学&quot;]

    A2A --&gt; P1[&quot;1️⃣ Event-Driven Architecture&lt;br\u002F&gt;事件驱动&quot;]
    A2A --&gt; P2[&quot;2️⃣ Stateful Task Management&lt;br\u002F&gt;有状态任务管理&quot;]
    A2A --&gt; P3[&quot;3️⃣ HTTP + SSE Hybrid Transport&lt;br\u002F&gt;混合传输&quot;]

    P1 --&gt; P1A[&quot;通过 EventBus 实现松耦合&quot;]
    P1 --&gt; P1B[&quot;Agent 只需订阅感兴趣的事件&quot;]
    P1 --&gt; P1C[&quot;支持流式和实时状态更新&quot;]

    P2 --&gt; P2A[&quot;任务可持久化和恢复&quot;]
    P2 --&gt; P2B[&quot;完整的状态转换历史&quot;]
    P2 --&gt; P2C[&quot;支持长时间运行的复杂任务&quot;]

    P3 --&gt; P3A[&quot;HTTP 用于 Request\u002FResponse&quot;]
    P3 --&gt; P3B[&quot;SSE 用于实时事件推送&quot;]
    P3 --&gt; P3C[&quot;天然支持跨网络的 Agent 协作&quot;]

    style A2A fill:#e1f5fe,stroke:#01579b,stroke-width:3px
    style P1 fill:#fff3e0,stroke:#e65100
    style P2 fill:#f3e5f5,stroke:#4a148c
    style P3 fill:#e8f5e9,stroke:#1b5e20</code></pre>
<h4 id="为什么需要-a2a"><strong>为什么需要 A2A？</strong></h4>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>场景</th>
<th>传统方案的痛点</th>
<th>A2A 的解决方案</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>Multi-Agent 协作</strong></td>
<td>每个 Agent 使用私有 API，无法互操作</td>
<td>统一的 AgentCard + Task API</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>长时间任务</strong></td>
<td>同步调用易超时，状态无法追踪</td>
<td>异步 Task + 状态机管理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>实时反馈</strong></td>
<td>只能轮询或等待最终结果</td>
<td>SSE 流式推送中间状态</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Agent 发现</strong></td>
<td>硬编码 Agent 地址和能力</td>
<td>AgentCard 动态发现和能力协商</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 id="41-a2a-核心架构组件">4.1 A2A 核心架构组件</h3>
<h4 id="1-agentcard---agent-身份与能力声明"><strong>1. AgentCard - Agent
身份与能力声明</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb17"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb17-1"><a href="#cb17-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F packages\u002Fa2a<span class="op">-</span>server\u002Fsrc\u002Fhttp\u002Fapp<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">ts</span></span>
<span id="cb17-2"><a href="#cb17-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> agentCard<span class="op">:</span> AgentCard <span class="op">=</span> {</span>
<span id="cb17-3"><a href="#cb17-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;Gemini SDLC Agent&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-4"><a href="#cb17-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  description<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;Code generation agent with streaming support&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-5"><a href="#cb17-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  url<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;http:</span><span class="sc">\u002F\u002F</span><span class="st">localhost:41242</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-6"><a href="#cb17-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  protocolVersion<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;0.3.0&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-7"><a href="#cb17-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb17-8"><a href="#cb17-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  capabilities<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb17-9"><a href="#cb17-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    streaming<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">true</span><span class="op">,</span>              \u002F\u002F 支持流式输出</span>
<span id="cb17-10"><a href="#cb17-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    pushNotifications<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">false</span><span class="op">,</span>     \u002F\u002F 不支持推送</span>
<span id="cb17-11"><a href="#cb17-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    stateTransitionHistory<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">true</span>  \u002F\u002F 支持状态历史</span>
<span id="cb17-12"><a href="#cb17-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-13"><a href="#cb17-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb17-14"><a href="#cb17-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  skills<span class="op">:</span> [</span>
<span id="cb17-15"><a href="#cb17-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    {</span>
<span id="cb17-16"><a href="#cb17-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      id<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;code_generation&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-17"><a href="#cb17-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;Code Generation&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-18"><a href="#cb17-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      description<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;Generate code from natural language&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-19"><a href="#cb17-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      tags<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;code&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="st">&#39;development&#39;</span>]<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-20"><a href="#cb17-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      inputModes<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;text&#39;</span>]<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-21"><a href="#cb17-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      outputModes<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;text&#39;</span>]<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-22"><a href="#cb17-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      examples<span class="op">:</span> [</span>
<span id="cb17-23"><a href="#cb17-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="st">&#39;Write a Python function to calculate fibonacci&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb17-24"><a href="#cb17-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="st">&#39;Create a REST API with authentication&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb17-25"><a href="#cb17-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      ]</span>
<span id="cb17-26"><a href="#cb17-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb17-27"><a href="#cb17-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  ]</span>
<span id="cb17-28"><a href="#cb17-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>AgentCard 的关键字段解析</strong>:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>字段</th>
<th>作用</th>
<th>示例值</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>name</code></td>
<td>Agent 的唯一标识符</td>
<td>"Gemini SDLC Agent"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>url</code></td>
<td>Agent 的 HTTP 端点</td>
<td>"<a
href="http:\u002F\u002Flocalhost:41242\u002F">http:\u002F\u002Flocalhost:41242\u002F</a>"</td>
</tr>

<td><code>true</code></td>

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h4 id="2-任务状态机---生命周期管理"><strong>2. 任务状态机 -
生命周期管理</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb18"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb18-1"><a href="#cb18-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F 基于 @a2a<span class="op">-</span>js\u002Fsdk 的 TaskState</span>
<span id="cb18-2"><a href="#cb18-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">type</span> TaskState <span class="op">=</span></span>
<span id="cb18-3"><a href="#cb18-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="op">|</span> <span class="st">&#39;submitted&#39;</span>       \u002F\u002F 已提交</span>
<span id="cb18-4"><a href="#cb18-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="op">|</span> <span class="st">&#39;working&#39;</span>         \u002F\u002F 执行中</span>
<span id="cb18-5"><a href="#cb18-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="op">|</span> <span class="st">&#39;input-required&#39;</span>  \u002F\u002F 等待输入</span>
<span id="cb18-6"><a href="#cb18-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="op">|</span> <span class="st">&#39;completed&#39;</span>       \u002F\u002F 已完成</span>
<span id="cb18-7"><a href="#cb18-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="op">|</span> <span class="st">&#39;failed&#39;</span>          \u002F\u002F 失败</span>
<span id="cb18-8"><a href="#cb18-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="op">|</span> <span class="st">&#39;canceled&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span>       \u002F\u002F 取消</span>
<span id="cb18-9"><a href="#cb18-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb18-10"><a href="#cb18-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F 状态转换流程</span>
<span id="cb18-11"><a href="#cb18-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>submitted → working → input<span class="op">-</span>required → working → completed</span>
<span id="cb18-12"><a href="#cb18-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                    ↓</span>
<span id="cb18-13"><a href="#cb18-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                  failed</span>
<span id="cb18-14"><a href="#cb18-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                    ↓</span>
<span id="cb18-15"><a href="#cb18-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                 canceled</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>状态转换详解</strong>:</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb19"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb19-1"><a href="#cb19-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F packages\u002Fa2a<span class="op">-</span>server\u002Fsrc\u002Ftypes<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">ts</span></span>
<span id="cb19-2"><a href="#cb19-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">interface</span> TaskMetadata {</span>

<span id="cb19-5"><a href="#cb19-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  taskState<span class="op">:</span> TaskState<span class="op">;</span>          \u002F\u002F 当前状态</span>

<span id="cb19-7"><a href="#cb19-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  mcpServers<span class="op">:</span> MCPServerInfo[]<span class="op">;</span>   \u002F\u002F 可用的 MCP 服务器列表</span>
<span id="cb19-8"><a href="#cb19-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  availableTools<span class="op">:</span> ToolInfo[]<span class="op">;</span>    \u002F\u002F 可调用的工具列表</span>
<span id="cb19-9"><a href="#cb19-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb19-10"><a href="#cb19-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb19-11"><a href="#cb19-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F 状态转换触发器</span>
<span id="cb19-12"><a href="#cb19-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">class</span> Task {</span>
<span id="cb19-13"><a href="#cb19-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">setTaskState</span>(newState<span class="op">:</span> TaskState) {</span>
<span id="cb19-14"><a href="#cb19-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> oldState <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">metadata</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">taskState</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb19-15"><a href="#cb19-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">metadata</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">taskState</span> <span class="op">=</span> newState<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb19-16"><a href="#cb19-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb19-17"><a href="#cb19-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F 记录状态历史（如果开启）</span>

<span id="cb19-19"><a href="#cb19-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">stateHistory</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">push</span>({</span>
<span id="cb19-20"><a href="#cb19-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        from<span class="op">:</span> oldState<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb19-21"><a href="#cb19-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        to<span class="op">:</span> newState<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb19-22"><a href="#cb19-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        timestamp<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">Date</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">now</span>()<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb19-23"><a href="#cb19-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        reason<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">transitionReason</span></span>
<span id="cb19-24"><a href="#cb19-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      })<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb19-27"><a href="#cb19-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F 触发状态变更事件</span>
<span id="cb19-28"><a href="#cb19-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">eventBus</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">publish</span>({</span>
<span id="cb19-29"><a href="#cb19-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      kind<span class="op">:</span> CoderAgentEvent<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">StateChangeEvent</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb19-30"><a href="#cb19-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      taskId<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb19-31"><a href="#cb19-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      oldState<span class="op">,</span></span>

<span id="cb19-34"><a href="#cb19-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    })<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb19-36"><a href="#cb19-36" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>关键状态说明</strong>:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>状态</th>
<th>含义</th>
<th>典型持续时间</th>
<th>下一状态</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>submitted</code></td>
<td>任务已提交但未开始执行</td>
<td>0-50ms</td>
<td><code>working</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>working</code></td>
<td>LLM 正在生成响应或执行工具调用</td>
<td>数秒到数分钟</td>
<td><code>input-required</code> \u002F <code>completed</code> \u002F
<code>failed</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>input-required</code></td>
<td>等待用户确认工具调用或提供额外输入</td>
<td>取决于用户</td>
<td><code>working</code> \u002F <code>canceled</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>completed</code></td>
<td>任务成功完成</td>
<td>终态</td>
<td>-</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>failed</code></td>
<td>任务执行失败</td>
<td>终态</td>
<td>-</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>canceled</code></td>
<td>用户主动取消</td>
<td>终态</td>
<td>-</td>
</tr>

<h4 id="3-eventbus---事件驱动核心"><strong>3. EventBus -
事件驱动核心</strong></h4>
<p>A2A 的 EventBus 是整个系统的神经中枢，负责：</p>
<ul>
<li>📡 <strong>解耦组件</strong>：Agent、Task、Tool
之间通过事件通信</li>
<li>🔄 <strong>流式传输</strong>：通过 SSE 实时推送事件到客户端</li>
<li>📊 <strong>状态追踪</strong>：所有状态变化都通过事件记录</li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb20"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb20-1"><a href="#cb20-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F packages\u002Fa2a<span class="op">-</span>server\u002Fsrc\u002Fagent\u002Fexecutor<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">ts</span></span>
<span id="cb20-2"><a href="#cb20-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-3"><a href="#cb20-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F EventBus 事件类型定义</span>
<span id="cb20-4"><a href="#cb20-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">enum</span> CoderAgentEvent {</span>
<span id="cb20-5"><a href="#cb20-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  ToolCallConfirmationEvent <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;tool-call-confirmation&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>  \u002F\u002F 请求工具确认</span>
<span id="cb20-6"><a href="#cb20-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  ToolCallUpdateEvent <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;tool-call-update&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>              \u002F\u002F 工具调用状态更新</span>
<span id="cb20-7"><a href="#cb20-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  TextContentEvent <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;text-content&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>                     \u002F\u002F LLM 生成的文本</span>
<span id="cb20-8"><a href="#cb20-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  StateChangeEvent <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;state-change&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>                     \u002F\u002F 任务状态变更</span>
<span id="cb20-9"><a href="#cb20-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  ThoughtEvent <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;thought&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>                              \u002F\u002F Agent 的思考过程</span>
<span id="cb20-10"><a href="#cb20-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb20-11"><a href="#cb20-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-12"><a href="#cb20-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F EventBus 实现</span>
<span id="cb20-13"><a href="#cb20-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">class</span> ExecutionEventBus {</span>
<span id="cb20-14"><a href="#cb20-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">private</span> listeners <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Map</span><span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dt">string</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="bu">Set</span><span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="bu">EventListener</span><span class="op">&gt;&gt;</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-15"><a href="#cb20-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">private</span> sseClients <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Set</span><span class="op">&lt;</span>SSEClient<span class="op">&gt;</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-16"><a href="#cb20-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-17"><a href="#cb20-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F 发布事件</span>
<span id="cb20-18"><a href="#cb20-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">publish</span>(event<span class="op">:</span> CoderAgentMessage) {</span>
<span id="cb20-19"><a href="#cb20-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">1.</span> 通知本地监听器</span>
<span id="cb20-20"><a href="#cb20-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> listeners <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">listeners</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">get</span>(<span class="bu">event</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">kind</span>) <span class="op">||</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Set</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-21"><a href="#cb20-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    listeners<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">forEach</span>(listener <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="fu">listener</span>(<span class="bu">event</span>))<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-22"><a href="#cb20-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-23"><a href="#cb20-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">2.</span> 通过 SSE 推送给客户端</span>
<span id="cb20-24"><a href="#cb20-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">sseClients</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">forEach</span>(client <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb20-25"><a href="#cb20-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      client<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">send</span>({</span>
<span id="cb20-26"><a href="#cb20-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        event<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">event</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">kind</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb20-27"><a href="#cb20-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        data<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">JSON</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">stringify</span>(<span class="bu">event</span>)</span>
<span id="cb20-28"><a href="#cb20-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      })<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-29"><a href="#cb20-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    })<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-30"><a href="#cb20-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-31"><a href="#cb20-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">3.</span> 持久化到数据库（可选）</span>
<span id="cb20-32"><a href="#cb20-32" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span> (<span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">persistenceEnabled</span>) {</span>
<span id="cb20-33"><a href="#cb20-33" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">saveEvent</span>(<span class="bu">event</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-34"><a href="#cb20-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb20-35"><a href="#cb20-35" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb20-36"><a href="#cb20-36" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-37"><a href="#cb20-37" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F 订阅事件</span>
<span id="cb20-38"><a href="#cb20-38" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">subscribe</span>(eventType<span class="op">:</span> CoderAgentEvent<span class="op">,</span> listener<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">EventListener</span>) {</span>
<span id="cb20-39"><a href="#cb20-39" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span> (<span class="op">!</span><span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">listeners</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">has</span>(eventType)) {</span>
<span id="cb20-40"><a href="#cb20-40" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">listeners</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">set</span>(eventType<span class="op">,</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Set</span>())<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-41"><a href="#cb20-41" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb20-42"><a href="#cb20-42" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">listeners</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">get</span>(eventType)<span class="op">!.</span><span class="fu">add</span>(listener)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-43"><a href="#cb20-43" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb20-44"><a href="#cb20-44" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-45"><a href="#cb20-45" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F 添加 SSE 客户端</span>
<span id="cb20-46"><a href="#cb20-46" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">addSSEClient</span>(client<span class="op">:</span> SSEClient) {</span>
<span id="cb20-47"><a href="#cb20-47" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">sseClients</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">add</span>(client)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-48"><a href="#cb20-48" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-49"><a href="#cb20-49" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F 发送历史事件（如果需要）</span>
<span id="cb20-50"><a href="#cb20-50" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span> (client<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">wantsHistory</span>) {</span>
<span id="cb20-51"><a href="#cb20-51" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">replayEvents</span>(client)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-52"><a href="#cb20-52" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb20-53"><a href="#cb20-53" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb20-54"><a href="#cb20-54" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>EventBus 流式工作流程</strong>:</p>
<pre class="mermaid"><code>graph TB
    subgraph LLM[&quot;LLM Stream 处理流程&quot;]
        Stream[&quot;LLM Stream&quot;] --&gt; Chunk1[&quot;Chunk 1&quot;]
        Stream --&gt; Chunk2[&quot;Chunk 2&quot;]
        Stream --&gt; Chunk3[&quot;Chunk 3&quot;]
        Stream --&gt; ToolCall[&quot;Tool Call&quot;]

        Chunk1 --&gt; Publish1[&quot;EventBus.publish(TextContent)&quot;]
        Chunk2 --&gt; Publish1
        Chunk3 --&gt; Publish1
        ToolCall --&gt; Publish1

        Publish1 --&gt; Local[&quot;Local Listeners&quot;]
        Publish1 --&gt; SSE[&quot;SSE Clients&lt;br\u002F&gt;(实时推送)&quot;]
        Publish1 --&gt; Persist[&quot;Persistence Layer&quot;]

        style LLM fill:#e3f2fd,stroke:#1565c0
    end

    subgraph Tool[&quot;Tool Execution 处理流程&quot;]
        ToolExec[&quot;Tool Execution&quot;] --&gt; ConfReq[&quot;Confirmation Request&quot;]
        ConfReq --&gt; Publish2[&quot;EventBus.publish()&quot;]

        UserApproval[&quot;User Approval&quot;] --&gt; SetState[&quot;setState(working)&quot;]

        ToolResult[&quot;Tool Result&quot;] --&gt; Publish3[&quot;EventBus.publish()&quot;]

        style Tool fill:#fff3e0,stroke:#e65100
    end

    style Publish1 fill:#c8e6c9,stroke:#2e7d32
    style Publish2 fill:#c8e6c9,stroke:#2e7d32
    style Publish3 fill:#c8e6c9,stroke:#2e7d32</code></pre>
<h4 id="4-核心执行器---编排引擎"><strong>4. 核心执行器 -
编排引擎</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb22"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb22-1"><a href="#cb22-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F packages\u002Fa2a<span class="op">-</span>server\u002Fsrc\u002Fagent\u002Fexecutor<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">ts</span></span>
<span id="cb22-2"><a href="#cb22-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="im">export</span> <span class="kw">class</span> CoderAgentExecutor <span class="kw">implements</span> AgentExecutor {</span>
<span id="cb22-3"><a href="#cb22-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="fu">execute</span>(requestContext<span class="op">:</span> RequestContext<span class="op">,</span> eventBus<span class="op">:</span> ExecutionEventBus) {</span>
<span id="cb22-4"><a href="#cb22-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> { userMessage<span class="op">,</span> task } <span class="op">=</span> requestContext<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-5"><a href="#cb22-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb22-6"><a href="#cb22-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">1.</span> 获取或创建任务</span>
<span id="cb22-7"><a href="#cb22-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">let</span> wrapper <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">tasks</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">get</span>(taskId) <span class="op">||</span> <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">createTask</span>(taskId)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-8"><a href="#cb22-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb22-9"><a href="#cb22-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">2.</span> 设置状态为 working</span>

<span id="cb22-11"><a href="#cb22-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    eventBus<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">publish</span>({</span>

<span id="cb22-13"><a href="#cb22-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      taskId<span class="op">,</span></span>

<span id="cb22-18"><a href="#cb22-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">3.</span> 调用 LLM</span>

<span id="cb22-22"><a href="#cb22-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    )<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-23"><a href="#cb22-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>

<span id="cb22-25"><a href="#cb22-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">for</span> <span class="cf">await</span> (<span class="kw">const</span> <span class="bu">event</span> <span class="kw">of</span> agentEvents) {</span>
<span id="cb22-26"><a href="#cb22-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="cf">if</span> (<span class="bu">event</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">type</span> <span class="op">===</span> <span class="st">&#39;tool_call_request&#39;</span>) {</span>

<span id="cb22-29"><a href="#cb22-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      } <span class="cf">else</span> <span class="cf">if</span> (<span class="bu">event</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">type</span> <span class="op">===</span> <span class="st">&#39;content&#39;</span>) {</span>

<span id="cb22-32"><a href="#cb22-32" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          kind<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;status-update&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb22-33"><a href="#cb22-33" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          status<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb22-34"><a href="#cb22-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            state<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;working&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb22-35"><a href="#cb22-35" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            message<span class="op">:</span> { parts<span class="op">:</span> [{ kind<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;text&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span> text<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">event</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">content</span> }] }</span>
<span id="cb22-36"><a href="#cb22-36" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          }</span>
<span id="cb22-37"><a href="#cb22-37" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        })<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb22-40"><a href="#cb22-40" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb22-41"><a href="#cb22-41" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    \u002F\u002F <span class="fl">5.</span> 等待工具执行完成</span>
<span id="cb22-42"><a href="#cb22-42" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">await</span> wrapper<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">task</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">waitForPendingTools</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb22-45"><a href="#cb22-45" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    wrapper<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">task</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">setTaskState</span>(<span class="st">&#39;input-required&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-46"><a href="#cb22-46" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    eventBus<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">publish</span>({</span>
<span id="cb22-47"><a href="#cb22-47" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      kind<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;status-update&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb22-48"><a href="#cb22-48" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      status<span class="op">:</span> { state<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;input-required&#39;</span> }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb22-49"><a href="#cb22-49" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      final<span class="op">:</span> <span class="kw">true</span></span>
<span id="cb22-50"><a href="#cb22-50" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    })<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-51"><a href="#cb22-51" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb22-52"><a href="#cb22-52" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>执行器的核心职责</strong>:</p>
<ol type="1">
<li>📝 <strong>任务生命周期管理</strong>：从 submitted
到终态的完整流程控制</li>
<li>🔄 <strong>流式响应处理</strong>：实时处理 LLM 的 streaming
output</li>
<li>🛠️ <strong>工具调度编排</strong>：管理并发的工具调用请求</li>
<li>📡 <strong>事件发布</strong>：将所有状态变化通过 EventBus 广播</li>
<li>💾 <strong>状态持久化</strong>：支持任务暂停和恢复</li>
</ol>
<h4 id="5-tool-scheduling---工具调度机制"><strong>5. Tool Scheduling -
工具调度机制</strong></h4>
<p>A2A 的工具调度是其核心能力之一，支持：</p>
<ul>
<li>⚡ <strong>并发执行</strong>：多个工具可以并行调用</li>
<li>🔄 <strong>依赖管理</strong>：自动处理工具间的依赖关系</li>
<li>⏸️ <strong>暂停\u002F恢复</strong>：可以中断工具执行并稍后恢复</li>
</ul>
