<h2 id="十给开发者的建议">十、给开发者的建议</h2>
<h3 id="101-选择-mcp-还是-acp">10.1 选择 MCP 还是 ACP？</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>如果你需要...</th>
<th>推荐协议</th>
<th>理由</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>为 Agent 添加外部工具能力</td>
<td><strong>MCP</strong></td>
<td>成熟的工具发现和调用机制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>构建多 Agent 协作系统</td>
<td><strong>ACP\u002FA2A</strong></td>
<td>原生的 Agent 间通信支持</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>企业级合规和审计</td>
<td><strong>Codex SQ\u002FEQ</strong></td>
<td>完整的审批流程和状态追踪</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>快速原型开发</td>
<td><strong>MCP</strong></td>
<td>丰富的社区工具和示例</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>高性能生产环境</td>
<td><strong>Codex (Rust)</strong></td>
<td>低延迟、低内存占用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 id="102-最佳实践">10.2 最佳实践</h3>
<h4 id="1-mcp-server-开发"><strong>1. MCP Server 开发</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb55"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb55-1"><a href="#cb55-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F ✅ 好的实践</span>
<span id="cb55-2"><a href="#cb55-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="im">import</span> { <span class="bu">Server</span> } <span class="im">from</span> <span class="st">&#39;@modelcontextprotocol</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">sdk</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">server&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb55-3"><a href="#cb55-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb55-4"><a href="#cb55-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> server <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Server</span>({</span>
<span id="cb55-5"><a href="#cb55-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;my-tool-server&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-6"><a href="#cb55-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  version<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;1.0.0&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb55-7"><a href="#cb55-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb55-8"><a href="#cb55-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb55-9"><a href="#cb55-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F 提供详细的工具描述</span>
<span id="cb55-10"><a href="#cb55-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>server<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">setRequestHandler</span>(ListToolsRequestSchema<span class="op">,</span> <span class="kw">async</span> () <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> ({</span>
<span id="cb55-11"><a href="#cb55-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  tools<span class="op">:</span> [{</span>
<span id="cb55-12"><a href="#cb55-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;search_documents&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-13"><a href="#cb55-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    description<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;在文档库中搜索相关内容。支持全文搜索和语义搜索。&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-14"><a href="#cb55-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    inputSchema<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb55-15"><a href="#cb55-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      type<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;object&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-16"><a href="#cb55-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      properties<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb55-17"><a href="#cb55-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        query<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb55-18"><a href="#cb55-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          type<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;string&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-19"><a href="#cb55-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          description<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;搜索关键词或自然语言问题&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb55-20"><a href="#cb55-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-21"><a href="#cb55-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        mode<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb55-22"><a href="#cb55-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          type<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;string&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-23"><a href="#cb55-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          enum<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;fulltext&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="st">&#39;semantic&#39;</span>]<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-24"><a href="#cb55-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          <span class="cf">default</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;semantic&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-25"><a href="#cb55-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          description<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;搜索模式&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb55-26"><a href="#cb55-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        }</span>
<span id="cb55-27"><a href="#cb55-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-28"><a href="#cb55-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      required<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;query&#39;</span>]</span>
<span id="cb55-29"><a href="#cb55-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb55-30"><a href="#cb55-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }]</span>
<span id="cb55-31"><a href="#cb55-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}))<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb55-32"><a href="#cb55-32" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb55-33"><a href="#cb55-33" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F ❌ 不好的实践</span>
<span id="cb55-34"><a href="#cb55-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> badTools <span class="op">=</span> [{</span>
<span id="cb55-35"><a href="#cb55-35" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  name<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;search&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>  \u002F\u002F 名称过于泛化</span>
<span id="cb55-36"><a href="#cb55-36" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  description<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;搜索&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>  \u002F\u002F 描述不清晰</span>
<span id="cb55-37"><a href="#cb55-37" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  inputSchema<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb55-38"><a href="#cb55-38" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    type<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;object&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb55-39"><a href="#cb55-39" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    properties<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb55-40"><a href="#cb55-40" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      q<span class="op">:</span> { type<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;string&#39;</span> }  \u002F\u002F 参数名不明确</span>
<span id="cb55-41"><a href="#cb55-41" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb55-42"><a href="#cb55-42" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb55-43"><a href="#cb55-43" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}]<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<h4 id="2-agent-安全设计"><strong>2. Agent 安全设计</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb56"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb56-1"><a href="#cb56-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F ✅ 好的实践<span class="op">:</span> 最小权限原则</span>
<span id="cb56-2"><a href="#cb56-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> agentConfig <span class="op">=</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-3"><a href="#cb56-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  mcpServers<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-4"><a href="#cb56-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    filesystem<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-5"><a href="#cb56-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      command<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;npx&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-6"><a href="#cb56-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      args<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;-y&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="st">&#39;@mcp</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">server-filesystem&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="st">&#39;</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">workspace</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">project&#39;</span>]<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-7"><a href="#cb56-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      \u002F\u002F 仅允许访问项目目录</span>
<span id="cb56-8"><a href="#cb56-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      env<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-9"><a href="#cb56-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        ALLOWED_PATHS<span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&#39;</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">workspace</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">project&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb56-10"><a href="#cb56-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      }</span>
<span id="cb56-11"><a href="#cb56-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb56-12"><a href="#cb56-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-13"><a href="#cb56-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  execPolicy<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-14"><a href="#cb56-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    autoApprove<span class="op">:</span> [</span>
<span id="cb56-15"><a href="#cb56-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&#39;npm install&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-16"><a href="#cb56-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&#39;git status&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-17"><a href="#cb56-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&#39;git diff&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb56-18"><a href="#cb56-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    ]<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-19"><a href="#cb56-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    alwaysDeny<span class="op">:</span> [</span>
<span id="cb56-20"><a href="#cb56-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&#39;rm -rf </span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-21"><a href="#cb56-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&#39;sudo *&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-22"><a href="#cb56-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="st">&#39;chmod 777 *&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb56-23"><a href="#cb56-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    ]</span>
<span id="cb56-24"><a href="#cb56-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb56-25"><a href="#cb56-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb56-26"><a href="#cb56-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb56-27"><a href="#cb56-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F ❌ 不好的实践<span class="op">:</span> 过度权限</span>
<span id="cb56-28"><a href="#cb56-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> badConfig <span class="op">=</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-29"><a href="#cb56-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  mcpServers<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-30"><a href="#cb56-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    filesystem<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-31"><a href="#cb56-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      args<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;</span><span class="sc">\u002F</span><span class="st">&#39;</span>]<span class="op">,</span>  \u002F\u002F 允许访问整个文件系统</span>
<span id="cb56-32"><a href="#cb56-32" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb56-33"><a href="#cb56-33" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb56-34"><a href="#cb56-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  execPolicy<span class="op">:</span> {</span>
<span id="cb56-35"><a href="#cb56-35" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    autoApprove<span class="op">:</span> [<span class="st">&#39;*&#39;</span>]  \u002F\u002F 自动批准所有命令</span>
<span id="cb56-36"><a href="#cb56-36" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb56-37"><a href="#cb56-37" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<h4 id="3-错误处理和重试"><strong>3. 错误处理和重试</strong></h4>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb57"><pre
class="sourceCode typescript"><code class="sourceCode typescript"><span id="cb57-1"><a href="#cb57-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>\u002F\u002F ✅ 好的实践<span class="op">:</span> 指数退避重试</span>
<span id="cb57-2"><a href="#cb57-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">callToolWithRetry</span>(</span>
<span id="cb57-3"><a href="#cb57-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  tool<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">string</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb57-4"><a href="#cb57-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  params<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">any</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb57-5"><a href="#cb57-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  maxRetries <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">3</span></span>
<span id="cb57-6"><a href="#cb57-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>)<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dt">any</span><span class="op">&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb57-7"><a href="#cb57-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="cf">for</span> (<span class="kw">let</span> attempt <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">;</span> attempt <span class="op">&lt;</span> maxRetries<span class="op">;</span> attempt<span class="op">++</span>) {</span>
<span id="cb57-8"><a href="#cb57-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">try</span> {</span>
<span id="cb57-9"><a href="#cb57-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="cf">await</span> mcpClient<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">callTool</span>(tool<span class="op">,</span> params)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb57-10"><a href="#cb57-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    } <span class="cf">catch</span> (error) {</span>
<span id="cb57-11"><a href="#cb57-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="cf">if</span> (attempt <span class="op">===</span> maxRetries <span class="op">-</span> <span class="dv">1</span>) <span class="cf">throw</span> error<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb57-12"><a href="#cb57-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb57-13"><a href="#cb57-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="cf">if</span> (<span class="fu">isRetryable</span>(error)) {</span>
<span id="cb57-14"><a href="#cb57-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="kw">const</span> backoff <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">pow</span>(<span class="dv">2</span><span class="op">,</span> attempt) <span class="op">*</span> <span class="dv">1000</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb57-15"><a href="#cb57-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="fu">sleep</span>(backoff)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb57-16"><a href="#cb57-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">continue</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb57-17"><a href="#cb57-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      }</span>
<span id="cb57-18"><a href="#cb57-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb57-19"><a href="#cb57-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="cf">throw</span> error<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb57-20"><a href="#cb57-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb57-21"><a href="#cb57-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb57-22"><a href="#cb57-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb57-23"><a href="#cb57-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb57-24"><a href="#cb57-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">isRetryable</span>(error<span class="op">:</span> <span class="bu">Error</span>)<span class="op">:</span> <span class="dt">boolean</span> {</span>
<span id="cb57-25"><a href="#cb57-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  \u002F\u002F 网络错误、超时等可重试</span>
<span id="cb57-26"><a href="#cb57-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="cf">return</span> error<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">message</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">includes</span>(<span class="st">&#39;ETIMEDOUT&#39;</span>) <span class="op">||</span></span>
<span id="cb57-27"><a href="#cb57-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>         error<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">message</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">includes</span>(<span class="st">&#39;ECONNREFUSED&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb57-28"><a href="#cb57-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<hr />
<h2 id="十一总结">十一、总结</h2>
<h3 id="111-核心洞察">11.1 核心洞察</h3>
<ol type="1">
<li><strong>MCP</strong> 专注于 <strong>Agent ↔︎ 工具\u002F资源</strong>
的标准化，由 Anthropic 主导</li>
<li><strong>ACP</strong> 是 <strong>Editor ↔︎ Agent</strong>
的官方标准，由 Zed Industries 发布，类似于 LSP
在语言服务器领域的作用</li>
<li><strong>A2A</strong> (Gemini 实现) 专注于 <strong>Agent ↔︎
Agent</strong> 的互操作，是构建 Multi-Agent 系统的探索</li>
<li><strong>Codex SQ\u002FEQ</strong> 提供了一个完整的 <strong>用户 ↔︎
Agent</strong> 交互模型，强调安全性和可控性</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="112-技术趋势">11.2 技术趋势</h3>
<pre><code>2024          2025          2026          2027
  │             │             │             │
  ├─ MCP 1.0    ├─ MCP++      ├─ Unified    ├─ W3C Standard
  │  发布       │  - gRPC     │  Protocol   │  - 浏览器原生
  │             │  - WebAssembly│            │  - 硬件加速
  ├─ A2A 0.3    ├─ A2A 1.0    ├─ Agent Mesh ├─ Edge AI
  │  实验       │  生产可用   │  - K8s 集成 │  - 本地优先
  │             │             │             │
  └─ 碎片化     └─ 融合期     └─ 成熟期     └─ 普及期</code></pre>
<h3 id="113-给未来的思考">11.3 给未来的思考</h3>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>"The future of AI is not just about smarter models, but about
smarter collaboration between models."</strong></p>
<p>—— 未来的 AI 不仅仅是更智能的模型，而是模型之间更智能的协作。</p>
</blockquote>
<p>协议标准化是 AI Agent 从 <strong>工具</strong> 向
<strong>基础设施</strong> 演进的关键一步。就像 HTTP 成就了互联网，Docker
成就了云原生，<strong>MCP 和 ACP 正在成就 AI Agent
的生态系统</strong>。</p>
<hr />
